	<div class="skava-mini-cart">
				
		<script>
			$(document).ready(function(){
			    var customerShoppingBagCookie = getCookie( 'VisitorBagTotals' ), itemDetailsCookie = getCookie( 'kohls_cart' ), miniCart, splitCart;
			    var cartEmpty = false;
			    var isAnonymous = document.getElementById('isAnonymousUser').value;
			    if(isAnonymous == "true"){		    
				    if(itemDetailsCookie){
				    	cartEmpty = false;
					} else {
						cartEmpty = true;
					}
				}
				// Display shopping bag sub-total and number of items
				if ( customerShoppingBagCookie && !cartEmpty)
				{
					splitCart = customerShoppingBagCookie.split( '|' );
					if ( splitCart.length > 1 )
					{
						miniCart = $('#mini-cart');
						// Updates the subtotal placeholders
						miniCart
							.find('span.subtotal')
							.text(splitCart[0]);
						// Updates the mini cart header quantity section.
						miniCart
							.find('span.number-items')
							.text(splitCart[1]);
					}
				} else{
					miniCart = $('#mini-cart');
					// Updates the subtotal placeholders when cart is empty
					miniCart
						.find('span.subtotal')
						.text('$0.00');
					// Updates the mini cart header quantity section when cart is empty
					miniCart
						.find('span.number-items')
						.text('0');
				}
				$('#mini-cart .subtotal').each (function () {	
					  var normal_value=$.trim($(this).text());
					  if (normal_value.length > 7){
						  var trimmed_value=normal_value.substring(0,6);
						  $(this).text(trimmed_value+'..');
					  }
				});
			});			
		</script>

	<script type="text/javascript">
		function isNative() {
			var hasParam = location.search.indexOf("mobileAppUser=S") > -1
					|| location.search.indexOf("mobileAppUser=T") > -1, hasCookie = getCookieByName("mobileAppUser") !== "";
			return hasParam || hasCookie;
		}

		function isTabletDevice(cookieValue) {
			return cookieValue.indexOf("|T|") > -1;
		}

		function isMobile(cookieValue) {
			return cookieValue.indexOf("1") === 0 || isMobileDomain();
		}

		function isMobileDomain() {
			return location.host.split(".")[0].indexOf("m") === 0;
		}

		function getCookieByName(n) {
			if (document.cookie.length > 0) {
				var s = document.cookie.indexOf(n + "=");
				if (s != -1) {
					s = s + n.length + 1;
					var e = document.cookie.indexOf(";", s);
					if (e == -1) {
						e = document.cookie.length;
					}
					return unescape(document.cookie.substring(s, e));
				}
			}
			return "";
		}

		function setNativeCookie() {
			var domain = document.domain, numDots = domain.split(".");
			if (numDots.length === 3) {
				domain = "." + numDots[1] + "." + numDots[2];
			}
			setCookie("mobileAppUser", "true", "365", domain);
			function setCookie(c_name, value, exdays, domain) {
				var exdate = new Date(), c_value;
				exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate() + exdays);
				c_value = escape(value)
						+ ((exdays == null) ? "" : "; expires="
								+ exdate.toUTCString());
				document.cookie = c_name + "=" + c_value + ";path=/;domain="
						+ domain;
			}
		}

		if (typeof (suites) !== "undefined") {
			var multiSuite, standardSuite = suites.standard || "", mobileCookie = getCookieByName("mobile");

			if (isNative()) {
				multiSuite = standardSuite + "," + suites.native;
				setNativeCookie();
			} else if (isTabletDevice(mobileCookie)) {
				multiSuite = standardSuite + "," + suites.tablet;
			} else if (isMobile(mobileCookie)) {
				multiSuite = standardSuite + "," + suites.mobile;
			}
		}
	</script>
